  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2fd0824d-2ffe-490d-85f2-819167bdbf15'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

      $('edition_24805645').observe('prototip:shown', function() {
        if (this.up('#box')) {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});

      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_24805645').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_24805645').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;

            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });

  <u>And the moral of this rerererererereread is</u>
</b>: if we lived in a perfect world, there would be a Kate Daniels/Hidden Legacy <b>crossover series</b>. It would be called <b>Wild Magic Hotness</b>. In this series <b>Kate and Nevada</b> would meet, fall in 💕lurve💕 at first sight and kick ALL the villainous villains’ asses to oblivion <b>scrumptiously ever after</b>. <b>Curran</b> would hook up with Cornelius (because animal mage, duh), <b>Rogan</b> with Barabas (these two are meant for each other, I’m telling you) and <b>Augustine</b> with Desandra (I’m sure she’ll love his flawless plums and magically-enhanced pork sword). <b>Grandma Frida</b> would live in sin with Roland and <b>Penelope</b> would marry Doolittle. <b>Ascanio</b> would have the hots for Leon, <b>Catalina</b> would date Julie, <b>Derek</b> would succumb to Troy’s charms, <b>Bern</b> would fall for Ghastek, and <b>Arabella</b> would be on Baby Conlan/Baby B/Cuddles/Grendel/Bunny/Talon/Mr. Himalayan Cat babysitting duty because she’s way too young to be thinking about <b>Tactile stuff</b>. This series would be <b>the best thing since</b> <s>sliced barnacles</s> Kate Daniels/Hidden Legacy/Innkeeper Chronicles/insert anything IA here, and the prospect of new instalments being released would leave us <b>feeling like this</b>: <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1506244525ra/23999924.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In other words: <b>Same old, same old</b>.<br><br><b>P.S.</b> Rogan = meow.   <u>And the moral of this rereread is</u>

Just so that he can "<i>drive me nuts with sheer frustration.</i>" Oh wait, said dragon is already safely locked up in the high security wing of my harem! <b>It's so cool to be me sometimes</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496829387ra/22955622.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>③ I want to <b>be adopted by Nevada's family</b>. That would be <b>slightly awesome</b> and stuff. <br><br>④ I want <b>Rogan to want my bullshit</b>. <i>DUH.</i><br><br>⑤ I want to <b>be an animal mage</b>, and have my own ferret army. But several? <b>Oh yes, definitely</b>. <br><br>① <b>If you liked</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20705702.Burn_for_Me__Hidden_Legacy___1_" title="Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn for Me</a>, you are going to LUUURRRRRVE White Hot. Too bad you have to wait <b>another 6 months to read it</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480696070ra/21340793.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>P.S.</b> Quick message to those who think they know what TACTILE TACTILE TACTILE means: hahahaha. <b>You silly people</b>. Slight. Might. <b>Muahahahaha and stuff</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480584047ra/21325996.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>P.S. I love you too.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1088286483" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1088286483" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1088286483?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24883189-white-hot">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=buddy-reads-are-the-best">buddy-reads-are-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=from-author">from-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=that-bitch-is-cray">that-bitch-is-cray</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=it-burns-us-precious">it-burns-us-precious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=kickass-heroines">kickass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=betas">betas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=superheroes-superhero-like-powers">superheroes-superhero-like-powers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1088286483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer523986693603266870"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2017/09/review-white-hot-by-ilona-andrews.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a></b><br/><br/>The first time I read BURN FOR ME, I had concerns about <i>literally</i> Mad Rogan. I mean, yeah, he was effing hot, but when Nevada had to explain to him, over and over again, why he <i>shouldn't</i> (b/c yes, brat, we all know you <i>can</i>) kill people just b/c they annoy you . . . I repeat, I was concerned.<br/><br/>In WHITE HOT those concerns were answered, and HOO BOY, if I'd thought he was hot before . . . *chants* <i>Tactile, tactile, tactile . . . </i><br/><br/>Nevada Baylor has a rare gift in a world that pr</span>
  <span id="freeText523986693603266870" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2017/09/review-white-hot-by-ilona-andrews.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a></b><br><br>The first time I read BURN FOR ME, I had concerns about <i>literally</i> Mad Rogan. I mean, yeah, he was effing hot, but when Nevada had to explain to him, over and over again, why he <i>shouldn't</i> (b/c yes, brat, we all know you <i>can</i>) kill people just b/c they annoy you . . . I repeat, I was concerned.<br><br>In WHITE HOT those concerns were answered, and HOO BOY, if I'd thought he was hot before . . . *chants* <i>Tactile, tactile, tactile . . . </i><br><br>Nevada Baylor has a rare gift in a world that prizes magical ability above all things. In BURN FOR ME we learn why it's been kept a secret--for her own mental health and happiness--but in the second installment of HIDDEN LEGACY, secrecy becomes impossible to maintain. <br><br>Her first "mistake" is using her Truthtelling to find the location of a kidnapped child. B/c now they know she's out there. Then when a group of mercenaries attack her home and family (with tanks and summoned monsters and FIRE and shit), and the only way to get 100% reliable information from the lone surviving attacker is for Nevada to take it . . . <br><br>The more people who know about a thing, the harder it is to keep a lid on it.<br><br>And now that people outside her immediate family (who love her unconditionally) know what she can do, she's faced with their fear:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>People were staring at me . . . A couple of them gripped their weapons in alarm. <b>I had horrified the professional soldiers. </b>I looked at my mother. Sadness softened her face, her mouth slack. <br><b>It hit me. I was the monster on the street.</b> Without me, they would’ve questioned and even tortured this veteran mercenary. They would’ve done it with the understanding that he would resist and he wouldn’t have faulted them for it, because in their place he would’ve done the same. There was a twisted kind of professional courtesy about it all. But me, I didn’t torture. I broke his will without even breathing hard. Each one of them could see themselves in the mercenary’s place. I could make them tell me all their secrets and that was more frightening than Rogan stopping a massive tanker truck at full speed.<br><b>I’d never felt so alone in my whole life. </b></i>
</blockquote><br>But before it can swallow her whole:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Rogan stepped between me and them, his eyes full of something. Whatever it was—pride? Admiration? Love?—I held on to it like it was a lifeline. <b>He understood. At some point in his life he had stood just like that, while people stared at him in horror, and he must’ve felt alone, because now he was here, and he was shielding me from their judgment.</b></i>
</blockquote><br>*rubs fist over heart* <br><br>So even before we were given a legitimate explanation for the ease with which he snuffed out lives <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he never emotionally left the war <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I saw it. "It" being why these two were perfect for each other.<br><br>But as lovely as all that is, there is MORE to this story then a romance that gives you the swoons.<br><br>There is Nevada's hilarious family. Like her grandmother, the mechanic who can communicate with armored vehicles and who claims spoils of war:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“What is it, Hanh?” Rogan asked. <br>“She marked all of the ATVs with her initials!” Hanh declared. <br>“Because they’re mine,” Grandma Frida growled. <br>“She doesn’t get all the ATVs.” <br>Rogan’s face took on a very patient look. <br>“Yes, I do. I tagged them, they’re mine.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Her cousin Leon who commentates battle (and is not in fact a sociopath, I promise):<br><br><blockquote>
<i>“I’m a veteran badass. I’ve seen bad shit. I’ve done bad shit. I’ve survived five months in a jungle eating pinecones and killing terrorists with a pair of old chopsticks. I’m one bad motherfucker.” <br></i>Behind me Rogan laughed. <i><br>“I’ve got two days to retirement. After I kill everyone here, I’ll go to my retirement party. They’ll serve shrimp on crackers and give me a gold watch, and then, I’m going to have my midlife crisis and buy a Porsche and . . . Oh shit, my head just exploded.”</i>
</blockquote><br>And that, my friends, is only the beginning. <br><br><b>Things you learn in WHITE HOT: </b><br><br>1. Nevada is not the only magically gifted Baylor girl.<br><br>2. Rogan's mysteriously mysterious background, both military and family.<br><br>3. Mr. Baylor's mysteriously mysterious family. <br><br>And that's just off the top of my head.<br><br>This is the third time I've read WHITE HOT (I beta read it twice last summer) and it will not be the last. This series has everything: romance, family, hilarity, a compelling story, a well-crafted and interesting world, GAH. I will come back to it over and over again, b/c it makes me FEEL things. When the villains are willing to sacrifice children as a means to an end, my RAGE is tangible. My heart breaks for Nevada when fear and ignorance make her feel like an abomination, and for Leon who believes himself mediocre in a family of exceptionals, I'm giddy as I watch Rogan pursue the woman he sees as living sunlight in a world of darkness, and a hundred other feelings besides. Not for the last time, I'm telling you that if you have not experienced the Andrews' worlds, you are doing yourself a disservice. They are the BEST. Highly recommended.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421060968i/13316940.jpg" alt="Jessica Signature" width="205" height="101" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My other reviews for this series:</b><br><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/866512435" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1)</a>
</b><br><b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434251816" rel="nofollow noopener">Wildfire (Hidden Legacy, #3)</a>
</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="523986693603266870" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1094344721" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17037741419585353545"><b>3rd read just as good.</b><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1520192269i/25161626.jpg' width='400' height='218' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>4.75 Come Into My Lair Stars</b><br/><br/>I keep thinking that I'm going to write you guys a better review of this. But no matter what I say it will not be as awesome as the words in the book and the fantastic blend of humor, sexual tension and action. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442588485i/16256012.gif' width='400' height='253' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This was one of my favorite descriptions in the book.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>he had thunder on his brow and lightning in his eye. I never understood what that phrase meant until Rogan’s face demonstrated it for me.</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Yes I know it is just release day but it</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17037741419585353545" style="display:none"><b>3rd read just as good.</b><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1520192269i/25161626.jpg" width="400" height="218" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>4.75 Come Into My Lair Stars</b><br><br>I keep thinking that I'm going to write you guys a better review of this. But no matter what I say it will not be as awesome as the words in the book and the fantastic blend of humor, sexual tension and action. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442588485i/16256012.gif" width="400" height="253" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This was one of my favorite descriptions in the book.<br><br><b>
  <i>he had thunder on his brow and lightning in his eye. I never understood what that phrase meant until Rogan’s face demonstrated it for me.</i>
</b><br><br><i>Yes I know it is just release day but it is also reread day for me. <b>SO EXCITED</b> I couldn't wait any longer to share this book with the rest of the world.</i><br><br><b>Original Review July 2016 (from the beta)</b><br><br>Wow…wow…wow.<br><br>The Andrews do not disappoint. This book had everything I wanted and more.<br><br><b>The sexual tension was…</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380912294ra/3201574.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The number of times something Rogan said made me swoon…..3, 7, 9, 23. Actually so many I don’t remember.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406275873ra/10528851.gif" width="400" height="166" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But beyond the Rogan and Nevada romance was such a fantastic story full of new magic. Nevada’s magic, her families, her enemies and Cornelius’s (the animal mage from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20705702.Burn_for_Me__Hidden_Legacy___1_" title="Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn for Me</a>) magic was amazing I want to have his powers because….<br><br><b>Ninja Ferrets!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468930404i/19760187._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="449" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ilona Andrews always comes up with some great monsters and we are not disappointed in this. There are some crazy beasties and a little more exploration of things that can come from the arcane realm.<br><br>This story had dark moments, romantic moments, cute adorable (Rogan with a Cat) moments, wtf moments, tense how are they going to get out of this alive moments and so much more. <br><br>But this still won’t be out for awhile so here is one quote to hold you over.<br><blockquote>
  <i> Enter my lair, said the dragon. I have shiny treasure for you to play with, I’ll keep you warm and safe, and if it suits my purpose, I’ll chain you to the floor and kill your client by throwing quarters at him with my magic.</i>
</blockquote><br>Full Review to Come Closer to Release Date.<br><br><b>Pre-Review</b><br><br>Everything else goes on hold now......This gets my undivided attention.<br><br>After my quick reread of Burn for Me I'm totally ready to beta this.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468465495ra/19709707.gif" width="400" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1116812633" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1116812633" />
    <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth"><img alt="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487525094p2/13870608.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1116812633?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1116812633" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17575694484575922452"><b>Maybe a gazillion ★★★★★ would be enough.... but probably not!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484762107i/21750939._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let's talk expectations. .. As all of us devoted readers know expectations can be the worst kind of plague. They make you excited and often a little bit manic and most of the time they lead to you wanting very specific things. Obviously the authors not being a mind readers can't deliver exactly what your overzealous imagination has come up with for their characters. And even if they could read minds, yours is probably not the only ove</span>
  <span id="freeText17575694484575922452" style="display:none"><b>Maybe a gazillion ★★★★★ would be enough.... but probably not!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484762107i/21750939._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let's talk expectations. .. As all of us devoted readers know expectations can be the worst kind of plague. They make you excited and often a little bit manic and most of the time they lead to you wanting very specific things. Obviously the authors not being a mind readers can't deliver exactly what your overzealous imagination has come up with for their characters. And even if they could read minds, yours is probably not the only overexcited one they would have to satisfy. But is this ever a problem with IA? Nope. Just nope. They deliver every freaking time. ... even their "average" books are only average when compared to <b>their</b> other books, and much better than most other authors' awesome ones.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485446526ra/21815536.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So now, having just finished this book (and I feel so lucky for having read this ahead of time) I actually have to write a vague enough review so that I don't spoil anyone's experience with this. Me... the Spoiler Queen!<br><br>So in very few words, what should one expect of this book...<br><br><b>Action </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485446526ra/21815537.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This should not come as a surprise since IA always deliver in this part. Fighting, car chases, magic duels, mythical creatures,... are IA's bread and butter and this book was no different! <br><br><b>Romance </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480184020ra/21282863.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series is more romantic than Kate Daniels. The first book had enough sexual tension to light a room, this one had enough to light a city. I am a romance kind of girl so was I annoyed by this? Not freaking likely! Especially since the emotions made Mad Rogan's and Nevada's back-and-forths no less hilarious.<br><br><b>Plot, story, writing</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485446526ra/21815538.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When has IA ever failed with a plotline? This book was one of the "Prime" examples of why I love this couple so much. This is a short series so these books are not stand-alones. I wouldn't advise reading them out of order. This book did have a short of beginning and end in the storyline but it was really only a part of the overall story arch. But there was no confusion or repetition of useless information. Everything was done so masterfully that you just kept devouring information and yet you were never fed up. The plot was complicated enough to keep you glued but not a tangled mess you couldn't make sense of. <br><br><b>Humor </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485446526ra/21815539.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Two words: Ferret spies!<br><br><b>Characters </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456680949ra/18266120.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Despite all the greatness of the above, we all know that the real strength of IA's books comes from the characters and their development. Both the main and secondary characters are always full of uniqueness and awesomeness and plenty of times crazyness. This book was no different. We get to know Nevada and mad Rogan grow right along with Nevada's family and their friends. We watch Nevada coming into her power and having to make difficult decisions, both personal and professional. We learn more about <b>my</b> Mad Rogan(*sigh*) and what makes him tick. We learn about her family and their unique weirdness. We get to know Augustine and Cornelius. Everyone is special, everyone has hidden and obvious depths and everyone is exciting in their own way. Even the villains are interesting! <br><br>This is as far as I can go without spoilers. Just read the book... it's worth it!<br><br><b>
  <i>ARC provided via Edelweiss! </i>
</b><br><br>*****************************************<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>OMG!! I got an ARC for this and Edelweiss didn't even bother sending me an email! I could have been reading this days ago!<br><br><b>*************10/1/2016************</b><br><br><b>2017? 20-fucking-17??</b><br>When did this happen and where was I? I take everything back. I don't hate the cover. I actually love it. I am just such a whiner! Just give me the freaking book and I will make this awesome cover a poster on my wall!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381579432ra/5062483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>**************1/8/2015*************</b><br><br>HOLY CHEESINESS!!! This cover is even worse than the usual for IA! WTH?? If I didn't already know them I would think they are writing bad erotica from the cover and even the BLURB which is annoyingly vague and too heavy on the promise of sexual tension to come.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438459666ra/15709943.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Meh...I can't believe I was actually looking forward to this cover.<br><br>**************************************<br><br>Aha... It has a title and a date(which isn't bad at all since I was beginning to think it would be 2016)!!! Well, it's definitely gonna be hot. It has <b><u>my Rogan</u></b> in it!<br><br>Now I just want a cover and a blurb.<br><br>**************************************<br><br>Another book I can't wait to get my hands on. Luckily though, now I will have at least 3 books from IA to look forward to every year.<br><br>*Dear book,<br>Do come out fast!*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/452703.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1354133159" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1354133159" />
    <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl"><img alt="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603085284p2/8734459.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1354133159?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl">Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062289261" href="/book/show/24805645-white-hot">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=r-rated">r-rated</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1354133159" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3122302923685452710">4.5 stars. This is a really great urban fantasy despite having maybe the worst cover ever. Review first posted on <a href='http://www.fantasyliterature.com/reviews/white-hot/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fantasy Literature</a>. Fair warning: Some spoilers in this review for the first book in this series, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20705702.Burn_for_Me__Hidden_Legacy___1_' title='Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1) by Ilona Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>Burn for Me</a>. <br/><br/>In <i>White Hot</i> (2017), the second book in Ilona Andrews’ HIDDEN LEGACY urban fantasy series, we return to a magical version of Houston, Texas, where some people (typically the rich and powerful) have inheritable magical powers. Nevada Baylor is from a not-particularly wealthy </span>
  <span id="freeText3122302923685452710" style="display:none">4.5 stars. This is a really great urban fantasy despite having maybe the worst cover ever. Review first posted on <a href="http://www.fantasyliterature.com/reviews/white-hot/" rel="nofollow noopener">Fantasy Literature</a>. Fair warning: Some spoilers in this review for the first book in this series, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20705702.Burn_for_Me__Hidden_Legacy___1_" title="Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn for Me</a>. <br><br>In <i>White Hot</i> (2017), the second book in Ilona Andrews’ HIDDEN LEGACY urban fantasy series, we return to a magical version of Houston, Texas, where some people (typically the rich and powerful) have inheritable magical powers. Nevada Baylor is from a not-particularly wealthy family that runs a private investigation firm, but she and some other members of her family have magical powers that are suspiciously strong for a family with no reputation at all as magic users. Actually, Nevada is a rare truthseeker: she not only knows when others are lying to her, but also recently realized that she can compel them to tell her the truth. But she’s trying to keep her magical power secret to avoid the trouble that public knowledge of it would bring.<br><br>It’s two months after the end of <i>Burn for Me</i> and the near-destruction of Houston. Nevada Baylor hasn’t seen Connor “Mad” Rogan lately, since she told him she wasn’t interested in a fling, and she assumes that he’s moved on, despite the intense feelings they felt for each other. Nevada makes a couple of fateful decisions: First, she decides to use her newfound power of magically forcing someone to tell her the truth, to compel a mass child molester/murderer to confess where he’s hidden the last girl he kidnapped, who authorities believe is still alive. Augustine Montgomery, who holds the mortgage on the Baylor’s business, warns her that if her abilities become known it could be dangerous for her personally, but she can’t stand idly by. Nevada takes the precaution of disguising herself for the confrontation with the molester, but she knows she’s taking a risk that word of her spectacular powers will spread.<br><br>Secondly, against her better judgment, Nevada agrees to take on an investigation for Cornelius Harrison, a gifted animal mage who appeared briefly in <i>Burn for Me</i>. His wife has been murdered while on the job as a lawyer for House Forsberg (hard to believe anyone would want to kill a lawyer, let alone four of them!) and he’s getting stonewalled on the details of her death. It’s clear that some of Houston’s magical Houses are involved in a far-reaching conspiracy. Unsurprisingly, as Nevada begins investigating Cornelius’ case, Rogan makes his long-awaited appearance. He has his own compelling reasons for being interested in this case ― as well as in Nevada.<br><br><i>White Hot</i> continues right where <i>Burn for Me</i> left off, with the fast-paced mix of adventure and romance that characterizes Ilona Andrews’ books. We learn more about the overarching conspiracy that endangers the life of almost every person in Houston, and Nevada and Rogan’s relationship continues to develop. The whole Baylor clan is back, as sassy and raucous as ever. Nevada’s younger teenage sisters, Catalina and Arabella, became more interesting and discernable personalities, and even are able to contribute to the investigation in some unexpected ways.<br><br>One of the highlights in <i>White Hot</i> is the role of Cornelius and his animals: he has a mental rapport with beast and can train them to do incredible tricks, though they’re much more than stunts. There’s a scene with some criminally-minded ferrets that is beyond cute. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480966018i/21369556.jpg" width="236" height="343" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As much as this scene will warm the heart of animal lovers, Cornelius also lets Nevada know that he has definite plans to avenge his wife’s death, though he’s close-mouthed about how he intends to do that.<br><br>The Andrews author team excels at world-building, and one of the more intriguing aspects of the HIDDEN LEGACY series is its delving into the genetic aspects of magic and the effect this has had on magic users and their Houses socially. Some types of magic are more compatible than others. Dynasties are built around particular types of magic, and marriages are ruthlessly arranged to try to achieve the best possible combination to have magically gifted children that will keep the House in a position of power. There are various levels of magical power ― Prime, Significant, Notable ― and a House without a Prime is no longer a recognized House. That, too, plays a role in the plot of <i>White Hot</i>, in more than one way.<br><br><i>White Hot</i> has a rather cheesy romance novel cover, which is actually fitting, considering that it contains a several-pages-long explicit sex scene. Personally I thought it was over the top, especially since both parties to it are massively beaten up and bruised and Nevada has two broken ribs at the time. Apparently the painkillers in this world are magical too.<br><br><i>White Hot</i> is a compelling, compulsively readable novel that kicks the HIDDEN LEGACY series into an even higher gear. The reason for the title of this series becomes clear in a way that segues into the plotline of the third book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27422533.Wildfire__Hidden_Legacy___3_" title="Wildfire (Hidden Legacy, #3) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Wildfire</a>, to be published in July 2017. If you’re a fan of the urban fantasy/romance genre and have any question at all about whether this series is worth your time, the answer is emphatically yes! … and you can skip or savor the long sex scene, according to your personal inclination.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3122302923685452710" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=hot-guys-alphas-rawr">hot-guys-alphas-rawr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-urban">fantasy-urban</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=your-argument-is-invalid">your-argument-is-invalid</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1139217857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3292231580422105773">I read this for the 2017 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-another-buddy-read' rel='nofollow noopener'>Machalo Group</a> Reading Challenge.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506286480i/24003492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Review:<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1496339108i/22902797.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Honestly, I expected this to be good, but not <b>
  <i>*this good.* </i>
</b> <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/953802752?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Burn for Me</a> was great, but this takes things to a whole other level. I'm putting it up there with the best of the Kate Daniels books (#3, #6, and #9 for me personally).<br/><br/>This picks up a few months after the first one ended. Rogan has disappeared from Nevada's life and she thinks he has moved on. Silly woman. Of course, their paths cross again when they get mixed up in the</span>
  <span id="freeText3292231580422105773" style="display:none">I read this for the 2017 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-another-buddy-read" rel="nofollow noopener">Machalo Group</a> Reading Challenge.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506286480i/24003492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Review:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1496339108i/22902797.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, I expected this to be good, but not <b>
  <i>*this good.* </i>
</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/953802752?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn for Me</a> was great, but this takes things to a whole other level. I'm putting it up there with the best of the Kate Daniels books (#3, #6, and #9 for me personally).<br><br>This picks up a few months after the first one ended. Rogan has disappeared from Nevada's life and she thinks he has moved on. Silly woman. Of course, their paths cross again when they get mixed up in the same job and firecrackers explode, chemistry sizzles... if you've read the first one, you know these two really need to be locked in a room with a big bed and STAY THERE for at least 3 days.<br><br>Nevada is still pushing him away because... dragon... lack of morals... dragon... the Scourge of Mexico... dragon... possibly psychotic... dragon... you get the picture. The guy is not the fuzzy feelings type (but he does get to hold a little girl's fluffy cat and that scene is just adorbs - sniffle). <br><br>So we're finding out there MAY slightly be more layers to Mad Rogan than he shows. Maaaybe. But only to Nevada. To everyone else: Dragon! Grrr. I hate you!<br><br>There is more romance in this one, so the cover is not way off in left field. However, this is still much more urban fantasy. The world-building is FANTASTIC. It just doesn't get better.<br><br>There is lots of humor and the supporting characters are fleshed out and play vital roles. You find yourself wanting to jump up and cheer, laugh like a maniac (okay, maybe that's just me), and even cry. (No, that was the mysterious invisible person - MIP - who sneaks into my house and cuts onions while I'm reading. Really, MIP, not cool. Not cool.)<br><br>If you're on the fence about reading "urban fantasy" and uneasy about reading a "series," I would say try this one. You have to start with Burn for Me, but it's worth it, and this one DOES NOT suffer from second book syndrome whatsoever. <b>
  <i>I promise.</i>
</b> (Did you feel the world quake as my vow was given? That was not gas!)<br><br>I have nothing left to give you but fangirling and squeeing and further embarrassing myself. I'm not ready to sell my soul to the Andrews like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah</a> did. But, I am volunteering as a minion. Or henchman. Or something like that. <br><br>Besides Nevada and Rogan, my favorites were:<br><br>- Nevada's entire family <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Finding out about the magical gifts of her sisters and cousins and how it played out was comedic literary history) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>- Cornelius and his ferrets<br>- Montgomery (the Ghastek of this series)<br>- Rogan's tactile gift which is a character of its own<br><br>Buddy read with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews Addicts</a> group.<br><br>(There is a cliffhanger, but the next book is out in August of 2017 or something, so I'll forgive.)<br><br><b>Previous posts:</b><br><br>Seriously, this may be the best book ever. I'm not even joking. RTC.<br><br><b>Before that:</b><br><br>RELEASE DAY, FINALLY!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br>Come to mama, Rogan...<br><br><b>Before that:</b><br><br>There's a cover now!!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427933078ra/14339258.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Looks like the publisher is still going for that cheesy romance vibe, though. What is up with that???</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3292231580422105773" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Where do I start?<br/><br/>This is the type of series that draws you in from the get-go, grips you the whole way, then spits you out all chewed up, wanting to claw your hair out while you wait for the next installment.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462097758ra/18952738.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>If you look at the GR page for White Hot, it's a slew of five-star reviews from obsessed readers who have considered selling their souls to Ilona Andrews in exchange for book 3. <br/><br/>So what makes Hidden Legacy so addictive?   <span id="freeText12297755321402483950" style="display:none">Oh boy. Where do I start?<br><br>This is the type of series that draws you in from the get-go, grips you the whole way, then spits you out all chewed up, wanting to claw your hair out while you wait for the next installment.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462097758ra/18952738.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If you look at the GR page for White Hot, it's a slew of five-star reviews from obsessed readers who have considered selling their souls to Ilona Andrews in exchange for book 3. <br><br>So what makes Hidden Legacy so addictive? I'll give my 3 biggest reasons real quick.<br>1. <b>The world</b>, my god, the world. Shaped by a multi-faceted magic system, it has incorporates fantasy into our modern world to give us a fascinating social system, power plays and political intrigue.<br><br>2. <b>Supporting characters</b> who are so creative and detailed, each and every one could sustain his/her own spin-off series.<br><br>3. An <b>antihero</b> you can't help but fall for. Seriously. If you're not in love with Connor Rogan, <i>what the hell went wrong in your life?</i><br><br>That, in a nutshell, explains my love for Hidden Legacy so far. If I haven't managed to convince you to pick up the series, then -<br>-first of all, you haven't read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20705702.Burn_for_Me__Hidden_Legacy___1_" title="Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn for Me</a> yet? What the hell?<br>-secondly, go read all the other reviews endorsing the series. We'll win you over eventually.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1496571067i/22928180._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Mwahaha!</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1822413421" />

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1822413421" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11201017722644342756"><b>Confession time: I'm a TOTAL <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/21748.Ilona_Andrews' title='Ilona Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ilona Andrews</a> nerd/super-fan!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497635810i/23045318._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='330' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When I met the writing duo at <a href='https://www.rtconvention.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>RT</a> this year and got a SIGNED PAPERBACK (<i>meep!!</i>), I just about died. I was saving the book for a special time because I LOVED <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20705702.Burn_for_Me__Hidden_Legacy___1_' title='Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1) by Ilona Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>Burn for Me</a> with a passion and I knew <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22303684.White_Hot__Hidden_Legacy___2_' title='White Hot (Hidden Legacy, #2) by Ilona Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>White Hot</a> would be a winner. So when I sort of hit a reading slump this week, I picked up that glorious paperback and got to work. <br/><br/>AND I COULDN'T PUT IT DOWN. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497636267i/23045361._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497636267i/23045362._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='330' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I stayed up until <i>3:48 am</i> finishing it! This is not a drill! </b> <br/><br/>Okay, I'll admit the book </span>
  <span id="freeText11201017722644342756" style="display:none"><b>Confession time: I'm a TOTAL <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/21748.Ilona_Andrews" title="Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews</a> nerd/super-fan!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497635810i/23045318._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="330" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I met the writing duo at <a href="https://www.rtconvention.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">RT</a> this year and got a SIGNED PAPERBACK (<i>meep!!</i>), I just about died. I was saving the book for a special time because I LOVED <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20705702.Burn_for_Me__Hidden_Legacy___1_" title="Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn for Me</a> with a passion and I knew <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22303684.White_Hot__Hidden_Legacy___2_" title="White Hot (Hidden Legacy, #2) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">White Hot</a> would be a winner. So when I sort of hit a reading slump this week, I picked up that glorious paperback and got to work. <br><br>AND I COULDN'T PUT IT DOWN. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497636267i/23045361._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1497636267i/23045362._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="330" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I stayed up until <i>3:48 am</i> finishing it! This is not a drill! </b> <br><br>Okay, I'll admit the book isn't perfect, perfect. But honestly, it's the most compulsively readable book I've read in ages. I literally couldn't put it down. It was EXCITING, romantic, abundantly entertaining, and just sooooooo damn good! <br><br>I couldn't stop <i>thinking</i> about it. I'm STILL thinking about it. I want many more stories in this world. I want all of Nevada's family to have their own freakin' series! I want more, more, more, MORE!!<br><br>Just awesome. Totally worth the wait to get the signed paperback by the authors themselves.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7715940177659464732">(Insert generic rant about covers.)<br/><br/>Putting my intense hate aside for just a moment, I do need to clarify that I loved the actual text of this book. I've gotten through all of the Kate Daniels series and the Innkeeper stuff, but I really ought to spell this out... I think I am in love with this series and it's even better than the others.<br/><br/>Sheesh. It's really a case of misleading expectations thanks to that damn cover. I mean, technically, it has a strong romance plot through it, but for the most p</span>
  <span id="freeText7715940177659464732" style="display:none">(Insert generic rant about covers.)<br /><br />Putting my intense hate aside for just a moment, I do need to clarify that I loved the actual text of this book. I've gotten through all of the Kate Daniels series and the Innkeeper stuff, but I really ought to spell this out... I think I am in love with this series and it's even better than the others.<br /><br />Sheesh. It's really a case of misleading expectations thanks to that damn cover. I mean, technically, it has a strong romance plot through it, but for the most part, it's magical PI stuff with an intensely powerful city-killer who's in love with Nevada, our main character... not, I should mention, the state.<br /><br />And even pushing that aside, we have wonderful character development, solid and near perfect progression and change of circumstances, and very cute moments with the family. What else could we need? Well, there's always murder, revenge, political stuff revolving the Primes, and multiple near-death experiences culminating in a really hot scene after so much cold... but that's just icing on the cake.<br /><br />It's a pure pleasure to read and you know what? As a UF, it's rather unique because it focuses almost entirely on a great magic system... without vamps or weres at all. WHAT???? A UF WITHOUT vamps or weres? GET OUT OF HERE! :) Seriously. It only rises higher in my estimation from here. :)<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7715940177659464732" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1096594147" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1096594147?book_show_action=true">Dec 08, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-kindle">books-i-own-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=edelweiss">edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=for-review-read">for-review-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-print">books-i-own-print</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1096594147" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1812357060481077491"><b>1st Read - 12th December 2016</b><br/><b>2nd Read - 15th December 2016</b><br/><b>3rd Read - 22nd April 2017</b><br/><b>4th Read - 26th April 2017</b><br/><b>5th Read - May 2017</b><br/><b>6th read - November 2017</b><br/><b>7th read - May 2018</b><br/><b>8th read - August 2018</b><br/><b>9th read - November 2018</b><br/><b>10th read - March 2019</b><br/><b>11th read - August 2019</b><br/><b>12th read - May 2020</b><br/><b>13th read - August 2020</b><br/><br/><b>Full Review</b><br/><br/>I do not have the words to say how amazing this book is, honestly 5000 stars would not be a high enough rating! If you enjoyed <b>Burn for Me</b> you aren't even going to know what to do wit</span>
  <span id="freeText1812357060481077491" style="display:none"><b>1st Read - 12th December 2016</b><br /><b>2nd Read - 15th December 2016</b><br /><b>3rd Read - 22nd April 2017</b><br /><b>4th Read - 26th April 2017</b><br /><b>5th Read - May 2017</b><br /><b>6th read - November 2017</b><br /><b>7th read - May 2018</b><br /><b>8th read - August 2018</b><br /><b>9th read - November 2018</b><br /><b>10th read - March 2019</b><br /><b>11th read - August 2019</b><br /><b>12th read - May 2020</b><br /><b>13th read - August 2020</b><br /><br /><b>Full Review</b><br /><br />I do not have the words to say how amazing this book is, honestly 5000 stars would not be a high enough rating! If you enjoyed <b>Burn for Me</b> you aren't even going to know what to do with yourself after you finish <b>White Hot</b>, it left me absolutely desperate for <b>Wildfire</b> so its a very good job that they're being released so close together.<br /><br />I loved every single minute of this story, the chemistry between Rogan and Nevada blows my mind, let's face it EVERYTHING about Rogan hits my hot spots - there wasn't a scene with him in it that didn't have me swooning and fanning myself! He's an intense, brooding, full on alpha male who is as hot as Hades and has a slightly vulnerable squishy centre that you only spot if you look hard enough.<br /><br />The world building was great before but OMG there is so much more to discover in this book, about the different kinds of magic, about Nevada's abilities and her family history, about the crazy magical creatures that can be pulled out of the arcana and even about the way the different Houses handle their disputes. I have to say that <b>Ilona &amp; Gordon Andrews</b> write the BEST female characters and families you'll ever come across. Nevada is so strong and kickass but she still has a lot to learn about herself and her magic and I love getting to discover what she's capable of right alongside her. Her sisters and cousins get their chance to shine in this book and I'm really curious to find out more about all of their different magical abilities in the future. I also loved the addition of Cornelius to the main cast of characters, his animal sidekicks are wonderful and the ninja ferrets are utterly priceless.<br /><br /><b>White Hot</b> has everything you could hope for: fun family banter, amazing chemistry between Nevada and Rogan, enemies who always seem to be one step ahead and who are willing to pull out all the stops to hurt our heroes. You'll be shocked one moment and swooning the next only to be watching in terror seconds later as you worry that all your favourite characters might not survive their latest adventure. One thing I guarantee is that you'll want to go back to the first page and start all over again the minute you finish it. I've already read it FIVE times and it's not even been published yet! I think it's safe to say that I'm addicted to this series, Ilona and Gordon were already my favourite authors but this series takes them to a whole new level and my obsession knows no bounds.<br /><br />I'll leave you with a couple of my favourite quotes just to whet your appetite further:<br /><br /><i>A tall man was striding from the far end of the hallway. He wore the black robe and it flared around him, the wings of a raven about to take flight. He walked like he owned the building and he'd spotted an intruder in his domain. Magic boiled around him, vicious and lethal, so potent I could feel it from 30 yards away. He wasn't a man, he was an elemental force, a thunderstorm clad in black about to unleash its fury.</i><br /><br />and <br /><br /><i>I finally understood why he was called Mad Rogan. It wasn't because he was insane. It was because he drove you nuts with sheer frustration.</i><br /><br />___________________________<br /><br /><b>Before reading</b><br /><br />OMG OMG OMG OMG I HAVE WHITE HOT!!!!! It's on Edelweiss peeps, go and request it now!<br /><br />I am crazy excited about this one and can't bloody wait to start it but I have a review copy of the new Innkeeper book to read first then I need to reread Burn For Me again (and no I don't care that I only read it a month ago!) but after that White Hot is going straight to the top of my TBR pile. I'm going to be in Ilona Andrews HEAVEN this weekend but I pity any books I try to read after this bunch of awesomeness LOL. I suspect a reading slump will be hitting next week!<br /><br />___________________________<br /><br /><b>1st read</b><br /><br />It's not often a book comes along that is so amazing that the minute you finish it you find yourself having to reread the entire series again. Considering I've literally just binge read <b>Burn for Me</b> and <b>White hot</b> in the last 2 days the fact that I already started <b>Burn for Me</b> AGAIN says it all really!<br /><br />___________________________<br /><br /><b>2nd Read</b><br /><br />No that's not a typo, I really did read both this book AND Burn For Me twice each in about 5 days LOL. That's how much I love this series - I am totally addicted and Rogan IS MINE!!<br /><br />It's far too early to write a full review so I'll post more nearer to the release date but I'm fully expecting to have read it at least another 5 times by next May LOL<br /><br />___________________________<br /><br /><b>3rd &amp; 4th Read</b><br /><br />I think I should give up on commenting after every read of this one - I did it again and read it twice in a week for the second time LOL. I can't help myself I'm just totally addicted to Rogan!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1812357060481077491" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Melindam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36434323-melindam"><img alt="Melindam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484595601p2/36434323.jpg" /></a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24883189-white-hot">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36434323-melindam?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36434323-melindam?shelf=uno-2020">uno-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36434323-melindam?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36434323-melindam?shelf=paranormal-urban-fantasy">paranormal-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36434323-melindam?shelf=cool-and-smart-heroine-hero">cool-and-smart-heroine-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36434323-melindam?shelf=never-judge-a-book-by-its-cover">never-judge-a-book-by-its-cover</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2014257245" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2713276357817872258"><b>5 Brilliant, Shining Stars - buddy-read with the awesome</b> <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa<br%20/>' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ilona Andrews Addicts IAA Group</a> <br/><br/><b>
  <u>THIS IS AWESOMENESS BOOKIFIED!</u>
</b><br/><br/>Reading felt like drinking this. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1495694792p8/3586543.jpg' width='300' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It promised a lot and OMG, did it deliver! It went right up to my head and made me feel fabulous. :)<br/><br/>Ilona & Gordon just went and did it again: reducing me to tears / laughter while making me hold my breath till the end and then of course serious deprivation, book hangover and the feeling of "IWANTTHENEXTBOOKRIGHTAWAY" set in. *SIGHandSTAREwit</span>
  <span id="freeText2713276357817872258" style="display:none"><b>5 Brilliant, Shining Stars - buddy-read with the awesome</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews Addicts IAA Group</a> <br><br><b>
  <u>THIS IS AWESOMENESS BOOKIFIED!</u>
</b><br><br>Reading felt like drinking this. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1495694792p8/3586543.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It promised a lot and OMG, did it deliver! It went right up to my head and made me feel fabulous. :)<br><br>Ilona &amp; Gordon just went and did it again: reducing me to tears / laughter while making me hold my breath till the end and then of course serious deprivation, book hangover and the feeling of "IWANTTHENEXTBOOKRIGHTAWAY" set in. *SIGHandSTAREwithtragicFACEintoHORIZON*<br><br>The story takes up shortly after the events of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20705702.Burn_for_Me__Hidden_Legacy___1_" title="Burn for Me (Hidden Legacy, #1) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn for Me</a> and it has a very strong and intriguing start. It reads just like a "simple" intro before we get plunged into the main action, but you just know that it will have wider implications.<br>Though Dina from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34593153.The_Innkeeper_Chronicles__Volume_1__Innkeeper_Chronicles__1_3_" title="The Innkeeper Chronicles, Volume 1 (Innkeeper Chronicles #1-3) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">The Innkeeper Chronicles, Volume One</a> stands closer to me in character, I love Nevada. She is still smart and strong, has high moral and professional standards. I also love every last member of her wonderful, loyal Family <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[from the maternal side anyway <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and was happy to learn more about them collectively and individually in this book, but of course I want more.<br><br>Rogan is as charmingly anti-social as ever and I cannot help liking him. He reminds me a bit of Dr. House: would probably drive me mad in real life, but is fascinating on page (on screen). <br><i>“Have dinner with me,” I asked. “At my house. You can help me explain to my mother and grandmother what happened to my work vehicle.” (...) <br>“Do you think your mother might try to shoot me?” <br>“Possibly.” <br>“Then absolutely. I wouldn’t miss it.”</i><br><br>The Enemy (whoever they are): their brutal and blood-chilling efficiency in pursuing their goals takes your breath away and they always seem to be one step ahead of Nevada, Rogan &amp; Co. Needless to say, that it makes the book even more tense and gripping.<br><br>I also loved the other secondary characters: Cornelius (his story just broke my heart), his daughter and his animals and especially Augustine. It is a wonderful touch from the authors: Augustine is an illusionist, always presenting a perfect facade to the world (I wonder what is lurking behind), yet he has absolutely no illusions about/to himself. Great characterisation! <br><br>World-building was taken up to a new level: the complexity of the magic Houses-politics, the role of Primes and the issues of magic + genetics were brilliantly developed and presented.<br><br><u>But the cover is even more hideous than the one before - utterly revolting. :D </u><br><br>Do you think IA was poking fun at their own cover with this?<br><br><i>"His (Rogan's) back and ass are one long bruise with a helping of concrete road rash, so his dreams of being a nude model are shattered for a while."</i><br><br>And this?<br><br><i>"Howling did a number on your (Nevada's) face, so you won’t be modeling in the near future either."</i> :)</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2713276357817872258" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2015341095" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2015341095" />
    <a title="Emma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8575414-emma"><img alt="Emma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1441431450p2/8575414.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2015341095?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma" href="/user/show/8575414-emma">Emma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8575414-emma?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8575414-emma?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2015341095" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8631628549828600603">If anyone had told me a few years ago, before I really discovered urban fantasy as a genre, that I could LOVE a book with a cover like the ones you find on this book and in fact the whole series, I would have laughed in your face. Judging books by their covers? Yep. Well please don't let the covers on this series put you off. These books are amazing! <br/>Nevada and Rogan are such fantastic characters. The romance is perfectly done, the magic of the world is great, the action fast paced, the plot so </span>
  <span id="freeText8631628549828600603" style="display:none">If anyone had told me a few years ago, before I really discovered urban fantasy as a genre, that I could LOVE a book with a cover like the ones you find on this book and in fact the whole series, I would have laughed in your face. Judging books by their covers? Yep. Well please don't let the covers on this series put you off. These books are amazing! <br />Nevada and Rogan are such fantastic characters. The romance is perfectly done, the magic of the world is great, the action fast paced, the plot so well thought out....how many superlatives can I get in one review?! I'm not going to say anything about the content because I think every reader needs to just enjoy it for themselves. But I will just say that Nevada's sister, Catalina, has an amazing and perfect magical gift!<br />And the book is laugh out loud funny in so many places. I just don't know how urban fantasy could get any better than this.<br />When I read anything by Ilona Andrews, (the couple of Ilona and Gordon), I always think they must be a great couple themselves: that there really must be something in the working together on their books, that makes the plots, characters, magic so good. They can be chatting out the plot gaps over the washing up or while taking the dogs for a walk. I think they must have a great relationship and family themselves to be able to write about them so well. I don't care if it's pure projection (don't anyone tell me if it's otherwise!) and I think that's pretty romantic in its own right.<br />Recommended.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8631628549828600603" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9665997869203105852">Re-read December 2019.<br/><br/>Yap, this makes me feel all warm and cozy. The breathtaking action is the spice on top, but it‘s about the characters and their relationships / interactions for me. The intense bits as much as the funny ones. All of it. Sooooo good. *purrs*<br/><br/>———————————————————————<br/>I'm in love!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488723239ra/22148126.gif' width='200' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498495957ra/23131857.gif' width='200' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This second volume starts action-packed and thrilling with the continuation of the conspiracy we learned about in the first volume. Nevada discovers the true extend of her powers - but, unfortunately, s</span>
  <span id="freeText9665997869203105852" style="display:none">Re-read December 2019.<br><br>Yap, this makes me feel all warm and cozy. The breathtaking action is the spice on top, but it‘s about the characters and their relationships / interactions for me. The intense bits as much as the funny ones. All of it. Sooooo good. *purrs*<br><br>———————————————————————<br>I'm in love!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488723239ra/22148126.gif" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498495957ra/23131857.gif" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This second volume starts action-packed and thrilling with the continuation of the conspiracy we learned about in the first volume. Nevada discovers the true extend of her powers - but, unfortunately, so do others. Connor has kept his distance, which leaves her with mixed feelings. But as grandma Frida put it, fate is throwing them back together (literally *lol*). It does so in the shape of a new case which, no spoiler there, is connected to the conspiracy.<br>So we have a learning Nevada that has to plunge into dark places (physically and mentally) to grow into her role; we have a chivalrous Rogan as intense as ever, who is trying his best to do what he considers best for Nevada; we have a compelling old-ish character that gets a bigger role here (though, at first, in a sad way); we get to know more about the single family members of Nevada; and we learn more about the conspiracy and its players. We also get to know more about Nevada's legacy and some "family" we hadn't known about (much) so far.<br><br>I like that Nevada and even Rogan show us that being just or fair or having principles doesn't mean you can't be hard and face your enemies with force. OK, Rogan might exaggerate from time to time *sniggers* but he's proof that even a tortured soul full of strength and a black-or-white view can be a good guy.<br>Grandma Frida was not as prominent in this one as in the first, which definitely impeded the humour, but we got more Connor and more Connor-with-Nevada which more than made up for it. *thinks of chapter 14 especially and starts purring* Besides, thanks to several other people, not least of all Augustine, there is still more than enough humour in this. <br>The further look into this society's rules (not only in Houston but throughout the US and even beyond) was something I very much enjoyed as well - not that the Houses are nice or anything, but the authors are just so good with world-building. <br><br>Now I'm in a conundrum: I flew through the first two books and therefore have to wait "a long time" for the 3rd (and later even longer for the 4th)!!! *wails*</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1108733951" class="readable"
