<span id="freeTextContainer9586208364511612383">4.5 stars<br/><br/><br/>I LOVE books by Ilona Andrews. <br/><br/>Even so I have read ALL Ilona Andrews books, I’ve noticed that her books get better while a series progresses. It rarely happens with other series, that the sequels are even better than the first book, but with IA it happens every single time!!<br/><br/>I don’t know what the secret ingredient is but their series ALWYAS get better with each additional book.<br/><br/>Maybe it’s the way they take their time, plan the series in advance, adding complexity and depth not only to the</span>
  <span id="freeText9586208364511612383" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br /><br />I LOVE books by Ilona Andrews. <br /><br />Even so I have read ALL Ilona Andrews books, I’ve noticed that her books get better while a series progresses. It rarely happens with other series, that the sequels are even better than the first book, but with IA it happens every single time!!<br /><br />I don’t know what the secret ingredient is but their series ALWYAS get better with each additional book.<br /><br />Maybe it’s the way they take their time, plan the series in advance, adding complexity and depth not only to the story but also to the characters. Who knows. All I know is that nobody can beat an Ilona Andrews book.<br /><br />In White Hot characters were more deeply explored, not only Nevada and Rogan but also their families, friends, co-worker, and the different houses were generously mentioned. With every book the intricacy of the story increases, more layers were added to the plot which in turn guaranteed a captivated audience – that would be ME.<br /><br />I fell in love with Nevada and Rogan even more than I already was. In book ONE I was fascinated, book TWO had me cheering – and in book THREE I was infatuated.<br /><br />By this point, anyone that has ever read an Ilona Andrews book doesn’t need me to tell them how it was, or what it was about – WHO CARES!!! It’s ILONA ANDREWS!!!!!!<br /><br />GO and READ IT!!!!!<br />For the readers that haven’t read Ilona Andrews yet, you better grab yourself book one and prepare yourself for an amazing and thrilling rollercoaster ride and the best Urban Fantasy of all.<br /><br />Enough said!<br /><br />Let’s read book 3 (which by the way I already did 🙂<br /><br /><br />___________________________________<br /><br />I received a copy of this book from the publisher for free in exchange for an honest review. My opinions have not been influenced by the publisher or the author.<br /><br /><a href="https://thebrowneyedbookworm.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more reviews and book recommendations on my blog</a><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebrowneyedbookworm/" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Bookstagram</a></span>

This is an unforgettable series with characters that will stick in your mind for a long time to come. I'm glad I waited to pick up this series so I am able to binge it now and not have to wait for my next f</span>
  <span id="freeText9088230780014466947" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars </b><br><br>It is time yet again not to judge these books by their covers! (God these covers are so bad). Another excellent PNR/urban fantasy book from the writing duo Ilona Andrews.<br><br>I'm going to keep it short and say while this book started off slow, it gained speed and by the end I was riveted. This is an unforgettable series with characters that will stick in your mind for a long time to come. I'm glad I waited to pick up this series so I am able to binge it now and not have to wait for my next fix.<br><br>Seriously y'all, you need to pick up Ilona Andrews if you haven't yet.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="9088230780014466947" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

This is precisely why I avoid new series. I have zero patience. If I like a book, </span>
  <span id="freeText9877666492642429697" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br> <br>God, I love this series. Especially that terrible cover. If it's depicting what I <i>think </i>it's depicting in this book then lawlz, because ain't no time for sexings when you're about to be dead. I'm not going to say anymore on that because spoilers, but seriously, L-O-L.<br><br><br><br>When I finished BURN FOR ME and found out the sequel wasn't out yet, there were tantrums. This is precisely why I avoid new series. I have zero patience. If I like a book, I want the next one in my hand, IMMEDIATELY, thanks, for the low, low price of NOW.<br><br><br><br>Instead I had to wait a month.<br><br><br><br>F**k.<br><br><br><br>And then I had to wait for the library copy to become available.<br><br><br><br>F**k.<br><br><br><br>Which it did. On the day I left for Japan.<br><br><br><br>F**K.<br><br><br><br>Luckily, I had the book for, like, 30 days, so I just saved it for when I got back and then literally as soon as I'd stowed all my travel gear and snarfed all that there was to be snarfed, I sat down and read this book in a single night - JETLAG AND ALL. After being awake for 36 hours, and then having one hell of an I-feel-like-death episode following the 16 hour time difference, I stayed up until 4:30AM PST reading this sucker, because <i>oh my God it was so good, I could not</i>.<br><br><br><br>I just reviewed CLEAN SWEEP and even though I didn't like that book nearly as much as this one (no Rogan, no tactile, no nada), I had to praise Andrews on her world-building. I haven't read anything stale by her, and the world in her <i>Hidden Legacy </i>series is no exception. In this world, certain humans have superhuman powers and are organized by House and by how powerful they are. The main character has the ability to tell when people are lying. Her love interest has the ability to have sex with people psychically. And also level buildings with his mind and kill people with quarters, but blah, blah, blah, that's not what has all y'all hollering. Let's be honest here.<br><br><br><br>LET'S BE HONEST.<br><br><br><br>Anyway, in WHITE HOT, people are being murdered and Cornelius, the animal mage from the previous book, comes to Nevada to help avenge his wife. Since the murderer might be a Prime (someone with the most magical power), they end up working with Rogan, too. Because pooling resources is good, blah, blah, blah. SORRY I CAN'T HEAR YOU OVER THE SEXUAL TENSION. So Nevada and Rogan are trying to figure out the conspiracy while also basically acting out the song lyrics of virtually every teenage pop song out there. So basically, I am like :D<br><br><br><br>:D :D :D :D :D<br><br><br><br>There's a lot of ARE THEY FINALLY GOING TO DO IT? in this book, and then a lot of NOPE, JK. And then finally, there's what's basically a chapter-long sex scene, because I think the authors felt bad for torturing us and making us wait a book and a half for these two to finally get together.<br><br><br><br>Is it worth it?<br><br><br><br>:D<br><br><br><br>If I had one qualm, it's that the world-building can sometimes be confusing. So far, it's great, just complex enough to be interesting and intriguing, but I do think that's something the authors should watch out for. It's easy to get tangled up in a too-complicated world and forget the details. But given the brilliance of these two, I'm not particularly worried. I bet this is going to be awesome.<br><br><br><br>NOW WHERE IS MY COPY OF BOOK THREE?<br><br><br><br>*moseys on over to the page for WILDFIRE*<br><br><br><br><b>"Expected publication: July 25th 2017 by Avon"</b><br><br><br><br>MOTHERF**K.<br><br><br><br>4.5 stars</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54721988-ha-fa?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2090219206" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6603099698516733828"><i>You can find <a href='http://novelnotions.net/2019/07/16/books-review-hidden-legacy-by-ilona-andrews/' rel='nofollow noopener'>this</a> review and more at <a href='http://novelnotions.net' rel='nofollow noopener'>Novel Notions</a>.</i><br/><br/><b><s>Second</s>Fourth read (don't judge! XD) - Spoiler-free review<br/><br/>This is a book I'll be definitely re-reading every time I need to go back to a comfortable, soothing, familiar place.</b><br/><br/>I honestly have no words to describe just how much I love Ilona Andrews' simple writing and colorful characters. Coming back to any world they created always felt close to coming back home and meeting with old and beloved friends. White Hot was no exception.<br/><br/><i>Okay, let's take </i></span>
  <span id="freeText6603099698516733828" style="display:none"><i>You can find <a href="http://novelnotions.net/2019/07/16/books-review-hidden-legacy-by-ilona-andrews/" rel="nofollow noopener">this</a> review and more at <a href="http://novelnotions.net" rel="nofollow noopener">Novel Notions</a>.</i><br><br><b><s>Second</s>Fourth read (don't judge! XD) - Spoiler-free review<br><br>This is a book I'll be definitely re-reading every time I need to go back to a comfortable, soothing, familiar place.</b><br><br>I honestly have no words to describe just how much I love Ilona Andrews' simple writing and colorful characters. Coming back to any world they created always felt close to coming back home and meeting with old and beloved friends. White Hot was no exception.<br><br><i>Okay, let's take a second to properly loathe and virtually burn the trashy cover that doesn't do the book any justice. Quite the opposite actually... There!</i><br><br>The story takes place 2 months after the last events of Burn for Me and Nevada accepts to investigate a murder case. Soon enough, she gets entangled in Houses' conflicts and a machination bigger than her abilities and ressources and powerful allies will be needed. <b>I found the plot to be much more compelling and immersive as the investigation got more personal and dangerous. </b>I was never bored. Not a single page. Not a single paragraph. I kept turning the pages while apprehensively checking the exponentially increasing reading progress on my Kindle. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>This wasn’t the world of normal people. Yet somehow I kept getting stuck in it.<br>“For the record, I don’t consent to being killed,” I said.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>I absolutely loved the way day-to-day actions mixed with frenetic high-speed car chases, thrilling fusillades and battles with arcane creatures, against a backdrop of shady ideologies and Houses politics.</b> Once again, I'm baffled at the amount of research the Andrews made on fire arms, cars, tanks and military. As a result, reading White Hot felt more like watching an action movie than reading a Fantasy book. <br><br>Nevada's development was pretty awesome and her struggle to maintain a balance between her duties, believes, desires and self-assertion felt incredibly real and easily relatable. I loved Nevada! I loved her hilarious family and their constant banter and meddling in her love life. I loved knowing more about Rogan and his complicated past and twisted logic. But if I'm being completely honest, the highlight of this book was the romance for me. <i>No, I'm not blushing...</i> Let's just say that it was very intense, swoon-worthy and <i>caliente</i> and we'll leave it at that...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450211347ra/17393483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780062674791" href="/book/show/32497873-white-hot">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Deborah by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/65798982-tessy-ijachi">Tessy Ijachi</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54790180-deborah-obida?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54790180-deborah-obida?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2169230236" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3727645023021547416">This cover is even worse than that of the first book, that looks nothing like Mad Rogan, that pose is just WTF! Can't decide whether this is better the first book, there was more action,romance and revelations but I kind of miss the whole mystery of book one. I don't know why but I always find it hard to review urban fantasy, you should read my review for the Raven boys, it was horrendous. I know that I've improve so I'll defintely do a better job here. The ship finally sailed here.<br/><br/>There was rar</span>
  <span id="freeText3727645023021547416" style="display:none">This cover is even worse than that of the first book, that looks nothing like Mad Rogan, that pose is just WTF! Can't decide whether this is better the first book, there was more action,romance and revelations but I kind of miss the whole mystery of book one. I don't know why but I always find it hard to review urban fantasy, you should read my review for the Raven boys, it was horrendous. I know that I've improve so I'll defintely do a better job here. The ship finally sailed here.<br /><br />There was rarely any new locations in the book, everything still happened in Houston, so the world building was the same with little improvement. The book is still written in first person POV of Nevada, I just wish its in multiple POV cause I want to know what goes on in her family member's head, despite my displeasure at the POV style, the book is well written, easy to comprehend and a fast read.<br /><br />The characters is my favourite aspect of this book, I love them all, even the villians here also has a sense a humour. So glad there was more of Nevada's family here than the previous book, Catalina and Leon's magic is finally revealed, can't wait to see what Arabella's magic is.<br /><br />I love this conversation so much<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“It’s terrible when he’s reminded he is human,” Augustine said to me. “He doesn’t know how to deal with it. Just think, Connor, one day you might be a father and get one of your own.” <br />Rogan stared at him as if someone had dumped a bucket of cold water on his head.<br />Payback time. “I doubt it. He’ll never marry. He’ll stay in his house and brood in solitude being cynical and bitter.”<br />“And entertain himself with his piles of money and high-tech toys,” Augustine said. “Like a broody superhero.”<br />Augustine had a sense of humor. Who knew? “Maybe we should invest in one of those searchlights with a Rogan symbol on it . . .”<br />Rogan reached into his wallet, pulled out two dollar bills, pushed one toward me and the other toward Augustine. “I hate to see comedians starve.</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_2271239124" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2271239124" />
    <a title="Maria V. Snyder" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1629797-maria-v-snyder"><img alt="Maria V. Snyder" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1530814046p2/1629797.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2271239124?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria V. Snyder" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria V. Snyder" href="/user/show/1629797-maria-v-snyder">Maria V. Snyder</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2271239124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7436665956370121637">I spent about 15 hours driving over the last couple weeks and I listened to this book. The narrator is fantastic - she also does Ilona Andrews' The Edge series as well (not sure about Kate Daniels). This is a great follow up to the previous book, but there were a couple times when I wanted to yell at Nevada for being a bit too stubborn - one of the things I dislike about most urban fantasy are the chip-on-the-shoulder protagonists, while strong, independent and skilled in self-defense/fighting, </span>
  <span id="freeText7436665956370121637" style="display:none">I spent about 15 hours driving over the last couple weeks and I listened to this book. The narrator is fantastic - she also does Ilona Andrews' The Edge series as well (not sure about Kate Daniels). This is a great follow up to the previous book, but there were a couple times when I wanted to yell at Nevada for being a bit too stubborn - one of the things I dislike about most urban fantasy are the chip-on-the-shoulder protagonists, while strong, independent and skilled in self-defense/fighting, they can be so stubborn - it's very annoying to me! Yes, they have good reasons not to trust and have built walls, etc... but there are a few writers out there that have the perfect balance - Ilona Andrews (yes, I know I yelled, but it was once or twice, not every other page!) and Patrica Brigg's Mercy Thompson series.</span>

<div id="review_1462574491" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1462574491" />
    <a title="Erin *Proud Book Hoarder*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder"><img alt="Erin *Proud Book Hoarder*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572373103p2/3048260.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1462574491?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin *Proud Book Hoarder*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin *Proud Book Hoarder*" href="/user/show/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder">Erin *Proud Book Hoarder*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24883189-white-hot">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=magic-powers">magic-powers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=part-of-series">part-of-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=got-in-2017">got-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3048260-erin-proud-book-hoarder?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1462574491" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11614426894246146007"><b>Original review below. Thoughts on this one based on a 7/22/2019 re-read. I hope Cornelius is in Catalina's book and doesn't disappear. There's something about the quiet character that interests me. And will we see the protective man from the party again? He was interesting. Ack, so many interesting characters and so little books/time. :(</b><br/><br/>4.5 stars<br/><br/><b> “I can be a good dragon, when the occasion requires it.” </b><br/><br/>The first book was my favorite read of 2015. To say I was excited for the two sequels to be r</span>
  <span id="freeText11614426894246146007" style="display:none"><b>Original review below. Thoughts on this one based on a 7/22/2019 re-read. I hope Cornelius is in Catalina's book and doesn't disappear. There's something about the quiet character that interests me. And will we see the protective man from the party again? He was interesting. Ack, so many interesting characters and so little books/time. :(</b><br /><br />4.5 stars<br /><br /><b> “I can be a good dragon, when the occasion requires it.” </b><br /><br />The first book was my favorite read of 2015. To say I was excited for the two sequels to be released in 2017 is an understatement. I couldn’t wait to get back to Rogan and Nevada’s adventures and romance, Ilona Andrews fun and inventive worldbuilding, and see what the author duo had in store for their appreciative readers. They’re definitely favorite authors of mine. <br /><br />This book opens up with two different openings – the prologue shows Nevada daring to use her talent, cloaked of course, to help the police in a particularly disturbing case to save a child from a predator. The first chapter opens where Nevada takes a case she doesn’t really want, moved by the man’s plight and financial struggles since he’s cushioned between two houses and their dangerous politics. <br /><br />While most of the book focuses on the first chapters story and mystery, that prologue plays into a personal disaster that rears its head later on, showing more on Nevada’s past, family history, and future issues with having to maybe reveal more than she wanted to with the public and her family.<br /><br />Character-wise, it’s awesome. Nevada is still a favorite heroine with compassion and determination. Her power is nifty but she discovers it’s advanced to whole other level in this book, which was a little wobbly. Rogan is as sexy as he was in the first book, and even if it seemed he was hiding out for a bit, he’s been changing things for Nevada’s life in the background. I finally get to see her sister’s power at the end in an exciting, intense scene. Her new client is fun and I was blown away by the ending finale when he deals with the villain who killed his wife. So glad to hear he will be staying around!<br /><br />Nevada’s family is still hilarious – the wedding photos taped to her door gave me some serious grins. I LOVE her family, which isn't usually the way it goes for me with large families already existing in books. With the grandmother, it reminds me a little of Stephanie Plum, although I'm not a fan of those books and family nearly as much.<br /><br />The romance is still smoking and finally Nevada opens her heart more to Rogan – seriously, who could resist? And yes, readers will be happy with their relationship in all the bedroom ways too.<br /><br /><b> “Maybe I should roll down the window to let some of the sexual tension out.” </b><br /><br />Throw in the series natural darkness with demented family politics and some creepy moments? Check. Toss in some serious romance and smoldering Rogan? Check. Throw in a detailed mystery with plenty of action scenes? Check. Top it off with more character development, more revealed about Nevada’s family, and you have another winner in the series. Seriously, read it.<br /><br />Why a small shaving off the stars to give it a 4.5 instead of a 5? There were a few developments that bugged me with how Nevada acted with her power, I didn’t dig the give-up attitude with Rogan if she had to do a particular thing in the end, and a few questions made me nervous. Overall though I have confidence it will turn out fine, which it did since I’ve read the third book before doing this review. All is well again in the end.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11614426894246146007" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1246622134" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1246622134" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1246622134?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1246622134" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer100360823554408393">The <b>Hidden Legacy</b> series is quickly shaping up to be one of my all time favorites. No surprise there, because in my opinion the husband and wife writing team that make up Ilona Andrews are so very talented! Thrilling plots, laugh-out-loud humor and romances that ooze sexual tension are the hallmarks of every one of their books! I can’t recommend their writing enough! <br/><br/>The Hidden Legacy series is set in a modern day Texas where people with magic powers have clout and are organized into family Hous</span>
  <span id="freeText100360823554408393" style="display:none">The <b>Hidden Legacy</b> series is quickly shaping up to be one of my all time favorites. No surprise there, because in my opinion the husband and wife writing team that make up Ilona Andrews are so very talented! Thrilling plots, laugh-out-loud humor and romances that ooze sexual tension are the hallmarks of every one of their books! I can’t recommend their writing enough! <br /><br />The Hidden Legacy series is set in a modern day Texas where people with magic powers have clout and are organized into family Houses. The more magical power you have, the more power you have. I break it down a little better in my review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/932766997" rel="nofollow noopener">Burn For Me </a>, the first book.<br /><b><br />White Hot,</b> the second book in the series, picks up two months after the events of <b>Burn For Me</b>. Nevada is pulled into a dangerous investigation when Cornelius Harris hires her to find his wife’s killer. She was working as an attorney for a private investigation company owned by House Forsberg, specializing in corporate espionage. His wife was brutally gunned down in a hotel and Cornelius is devastated by her death, and even though Nevada’s first instinct is to refuse the job because of the danger. But Nevada knows she wouldn’t be able to look herself in the mirror if she doesn’t help him. The investigation immediately turns deadly; underscoring the serious threat they’re up against. <br /><br />Of course, this series wouldn’t be as much fun if Connor “Mad” Rogan, didn’t somehow factor in, and he becomes a big part of the story very quickly! I was thrilled about that because the minute they’re in a room together the sexual tension climbs and the sparks fly! The hilarious sniping, clever banter, sexual innuendo is just too much fun! In spite of not seeing Connor for two months, his impact on Nevada’s senses is not dulled at all. Oh, these two could light my kindle on fire! Their relationship was mostly love/hate with a few <i>really </i>good moments, in the last book, so I was <i>so</i> pleased at the progress they made here, getting to know each other and the person underneath. <br /><br />Nevada’s family is super funny, as well. Her Grandma, the mechanic who assembles tanks, her mother an ex-sniper for the army, and her younger sisters and cousin Bern, Nevada’s information specialist, make for an eclectic bunch. Nevada’s grandmother and sisters tease her mercilessly about Mad in such an annoying way only accomplished by family! Many laughs there! I was happy to find out more about her sister’s magic powers, and now I can see why her family is so secretive about all of their abilities! <br /><br />Like I said, I LOVE this series. I I quickly read <b>White Hot </b>back in December when I received a copy, and I’ve just bought the audio since it released this last Tuesday and I’m “reading” again! So, so good! I’m dying to get my hands on the next book, which I think may be the last. Thankfully, I don’t have too long to wait because it releases July 25th! <br /><i><br />A copy was kindly provided by Avon via Edelweiss in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /><br />This review is also posted at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2017/06/review-white-hot-by-ilona-andrews.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="100360823554408393" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xUY0SX9E9qfBrYOPm0GVKl/J/WwPYh563RKapXc5ekbmvu6pd9SGYGjiUL7DO4vp39ICkch4pD9xH8Quoed5iA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CsPcjaVWp+KZr0YOrScxzX9IZlfYkdK9uy2ywI8sZTgpOwZtrcbXJTDglT/1XS8O/1OZqh+LaPgXIOxLWfJm9g==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13548790345915786796">Ilona Andrews is the pseudonym for a husband-and-wife writing team. Ilona is a native-born Russian and Gordon is a former communications sergeant in the U.S. Army. Contrary to popular belief, Gordon was never an intelligence officer with a license to kill, and Ilona was never the mysterious Russian spy who seduced him. They met in college, in English Composition 101, where Ilona got a better grade</span>
  <span id="freeText13548790345915786796" style="display:none">Ilona Andrews is the pseudonym for a husband-and-wife writing team. Ilona is a native-born Russian and Gordon is a former communications sergeant in the U.S. Army. Contrary to popular belief, Gordon was never an intelligence officer with a license to kill, and Ilona was never the mysterious Russian spy who seduced him. They met in college, in English Composition 101, where Ilona got a better grade. (Gordon is still sore about that.)<br /><br />Gordon and Ilona currently reside in Oregon with their two children, three dogs and a cat. They have co-authored two series, the bestselling urban fantasy of Kate Daniels and romantic urban fantasy of The Edge.<br /></span>
